  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_dc28b627-b3ec-4c4d-945a-28cf19ecacc1'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);

  <span id="freeText16947647899322265363" style="display:none"><b>A Song of Love won her heart.</b><br /><b>A Song of Darkness haunted her soul.</b><br /><b>A Song in the Dance would seal her fate.</b><br /><br />Seers had long foreseen an extraordinary destiny for Ellysetta Baristani. Already she had won the heart of the Fey King—the magnificent Rain, ever her ally, eternally her love. She had saved the offspring of the magical tairen and fought beside her legendary mate against the armies of Eld. But the most powerful—and dangerous—Verse of her Song had yet to be sung. <br /><br />As the final battle draws nigh and evil tightens its grip upon her soul—will Ellysetta secure the world for Light or plunge it into Darkness for all eternity? As she and Rain fight for each other, side by side, will they find a way to complete their truemate bond and defeat the evil High Mage of Eld before it's too late, or must they make the ultimate sacrifice to save their world?</span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3043482-terry-ter05-twimoms-mundiemoms?shelf=read-more-than-once">read-more-than-once</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3043482-terry-ter05-twimoms-mundiemoms?shelf=demons">demons</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3043482-terry-ter05-twimoms-mundiemoms?shelf=epic-series">epic-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3043482-terry-ter05-twimoms-mundiemoms?shelf=not-young-adult">not-young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3043482-terry-ter05-twimoms-mundiemoms?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer133895542" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11464502039964964843">[Second EDIT] I am not sure how many times I have read this series of five books - four or five counting the audiobooks. Each time I am just blown away, not just with this wonderful fantasy world the author has created but with the beautiful characters so different than any other fantasy books I have read. If this is not my favorite series EVER, I am not sure I can think of one that is better. Close...but not better. <br/><br/>[REREAD - SECOND TIME]<br/>Once again I have finished the fifth and last book in the</span>
  <span id="freeText11464502039964964843" style="display:none">[Second EDIT] I am not sure how many times I have read this series of five books - four or five counting the audiobooks. Each time I am just blown away, not just with this wonderful fantasy world the author has created but with the beautiful characters so different than any other fantasy books I have read. If this is not my favorite series EVER, I am not sure I can think of one that is better. Close...but not better. <br /><br />[REREAD - SECOND TIME]<br />Once again I have finished the fifth and last book in the series that I have to admit is my favorite ever. And that is saying a lot. This is a world and a story that it is very difficult to move away from. The world that this author has created is not like anything I can compare it to for several reasons. The Fey in these books are the most honorable beings imaginable. The men's respect for tradition, for each other as warriors (and they ARE warriors), their reverence and respect for women, as well as the incredible women who are all healers in some way is so beautiful. The Fey in this story are hundreds of years old at the youngest and in some cases have lived for 2000 years or more. The relationship with them, the humans (some of whom have fey blood), and the Elves is so well explained that I never was confused or unable to understand the connections. The Mages are as evil as you can get in a story, so this is a battle between Light and Dark. Major major wonderful writing by this author.<br /><br />I can't say enough about the love between Rain and Ellysetta and the love scenes between them. This is not a YA book and some of the scenes are explicit, but somehow they are so beautifully written I didn't cringe (have to admit I am not into graphic sex scenes). This kind of love is magic, beyond real, and pretty much sings a song of LOVE like few other books. Actually, like any other book I have read.<br /><br />I knew all along we were heading for a terrible showdown between good and evil, and all of the Fey I have come to love would be in terrible danger. I think the first fourth or so of the book was a little tedious for me because I knew it was setting up for what was to come. Then it CAME and I could not have put the book down had my house been burning down. <br /><br />This book is the darkest of them all, the most threatening to Rain and Ellysetta at a time when she is most vulnerable to the evil Mage and when Rain is fighting against the madness of the truemate bond that has not been completed (you have to read them to understand that one). The most beautiful part (well nearly) is when they they are saved by the dahl'reisen who have been reviled and banished from the Fading Lands for thousands of years. What happens then turns upside down everything that the Fey have believed in for milliniums. There are no words for the bravery, loyalty, and sacrifice that is shown by so many in Rain and Ellie's race to outrun their enemies. If one likes reading about battles, this book has it, and strangely this is something I normally do not like and yet in this book it all worked for me. I don't enjoy reading real dark stories and yet the evil in this book was necessary because Light only really triumphs when darkness is at it's worst. I am sure I was holding my breath more than once during that last half of this final book. Wonderful wonderful author. Beylah vo.<br /><br />I hate to say good-bye to this series and I am sure I will read it many times again. I even learned a new language - Feyan. </span>
  <a data-text-id="11464502039964964843" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer11353522360816989169">This review was originally posted on<a href='http://addictedtoromance.org/2017/07/24/re-read-review-the-crown-of-crystal-flame-by-c-l-wilson/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'> Addicted To Romance</a><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1500949594i/23398983._SX540_.jpg' alt='' width='600' height='100' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>In the final installment of the saga of Ellysetta Baristani and the Tairen Soul King Rain. This book sets off right after the ending of Queen of Song and Soul, where our wonderful Adrial and his truemate are killed. I am so grateful this was a re read, but man its been years and I had forgotten how much this author can pull me right into a story, and how easily I get wrapped up into these characters and my goodness...all the feels this seri</span>
  <span id="freeText11353522360816989169" style="display:none">This review was originally posted on<a href="http://addictedtoromance.org/2017/07/24/re-read-review-the-crown-of-crystal-flame-by-c-l-wilson/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"> Addicted To Romance</a><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1500949594i/23398983._SX540_.jpg" alt="" width="600" height="100" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In the final installment of the saga of Ellysetta Baristani and the Tairen Soul King Rain. This book sets off right after the ending of Queen of Song and Soul, where our wonderful Adrial and his truemate are killed. I am so grateful this was a re read, but man its been years and I had forgotten how much this author can pull me right into a story, and how easily I get wrapped up into these characters and my goodness...all the feels this series and especially this last installment conveys is beyond extraordinary. In  this book, we come to the final battle between the Celirians and Fey and the evil Mages who are trying to destroy all in their path. We such strengths in Rain and Ellysetta and all of those special people that protect and defend them. We see the true courage Ellysetta's parents have, suffering over a thousand years of torture and protecting her as best the can. Ellysetta has come a long way from a innocent woodcarver's daughter, to learning of her fate to be the Tairen Fey King's truemate and developing her gifts so she could heal the young tairen kitlings. And learning how to sing true song in many different ways and learning of her destiny that will either make her capable of destroying the evil mages or a power that will consume her and destroy the light within her. Ellysetta and Rain go through war, and strife, pain and suffering, but in this beautifully compelling final story, we see how strong they are together, and vibrant their connection is. <br> 
  
    
      <b>Let love, not fear, be your guide.</b>
    
  
 <br>There is something so magical about their epic story of love and courage, of seeing them fight together for freedom and love. It was simply a wonderful experience to read this series again, and when I realized I had yet to review this book, I knew I needed to do a short review because really this book definitely deserves it. If you have yet to read this series, or this author....you need to pick up this series...IMMEDIATELY. I guarantee it will make you fall in love with this wondrous world that C.L. Wilson has created and you will become captivated with all of my favorite characters including our playful and feisty Tairen's and the quintent.<br> 
  <strong>
    
      The Fey did nothing in half measures. That intensity of emotion was part of their appeal. It made them the fiercest warriors, the staunchest allies, the most passionate lovers. The most devoted mates.
    
  </strong>
 <br>This is a story that will leave you on edge, break through your emotional barriers, and tug at your heartstrings. This book and this whole series, stays with you and even though this is my second time reading this book, it has always held a special place in my heart and I know it will in yours too!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1500946354i/23398684._SX540_.jpg" alt="" width="600" height="100" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>

<div id="review_81211497" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/81211497" />
    <a title="MelissaB" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1320046-melissab"><img alt="MelissaB" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1245899832p2/1320046.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/81211497?book_show_action=true">Dec 16, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="MelissaB" class="user" itemprop="url" name="MelissaB" href="/user/show/1320046-melissab">MelissaB</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1320046-melissab?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1320046-melissab?shelf=shapeshifters">shapeshifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1320046-melissab?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1320046-melissab?shelf=cl-wilson">cl-wilson</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1320046-melissab?shelf=2013-reads">2013-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer81211497" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17665187166701547942">Crown of Crystal Flame is the final book in the five book Tairen Souls series where we finally see the battle between Light and Dark forces that will determine the fate of the world.<br/><br/>Ellysetta and her truemate Rain, King of the Fey, have been through so much as they battle the High Mage of Eld and his plans to conquer the world including the Fading Lands - and most of all his quest to capture Ellysetta. The final chapter of this epic fantasy romance is full of battles, adventures and the final sh</span>
  <span id="freeText17665187166701547942" style="display:none">Crown of Crystal Flame is the final book in the five book Tairen Souls series where we finally see the battle between Light and Dark forces that will determine the fate of the world.<br /><br />Ellysetta and her truemate Rain, King of the Fey, have been through so much as they battle the High Mage of Eld and his plans to conquer the world including the Fading Lands - and most of all his quest to capture Ellysetta. The final chapter of this epic fantasy romance is full of battles, adventures and the final showdown for Ellysetta to be Light or Dark. Along the way familiar characters are lost and we meet some new ones, the Elves in particular were fascinating. <br /><br />Looking back over this series as a whole, the story was wonderfully imaginative and filled with characters who came to life. The world building and writing were amazing, I felt like I was in a magical world similar to Lord of the Rings. I loved the first two books in particular, they focused the most on Ellysetta and Rain as they met and started their relationship. The third and fourth books were a bit too dark, I felt like there was little hope and bad things kept happening to beloved characters. Finally in this book we see the final battles and a brighter future. I was pleased that the battle with the High Mage was more than just him and Ellie, she has many people who cared about her. The final chapters felt a little rushed, I would have enjoyed more information on where some of our characters end up, especially the girl from Eld and the babies. We get to see our main characters and their happy endings so I am still happy.<br /><br />I would recommend this series to people who enjoy epic fantasy romance. The characters and story will stay with me long after I am finished.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17665187166701547942" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer7880242319570692159"><b>Final rating: 5/5 stars</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> “Let love, not fear, be your guide.” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/>And with this book, the series has ended. It was a nice journey while it lasted and i don't regret reading this series. Although, by the time that you start reading this book, you already know enough of what will happen in the future, thanks to prophecies and what not. Even so, it was interesting and well done story, but the best part of this whole story lied in characters.<br/><br/>I will miss all of them, and i will miss their worl</span>
  <span id="freeText7880242319570692159" style="display:none"><b>Final rating: 5/5 stars</b><br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> “Let love, not fear, be your guide.” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br />And with this book, the series has ended. It was a nice journey while it lasted and i don't regret reading this series. Although, by the time that you start reading this book, you already know enough of what will happen in the future, thanks to prophecies and what not. Even so, it was interesting and well done story, but the best part of this whole story lied in characters.<br /><br />I will miss all of them, and i will miss their world. Overall, this series is not for faint hearted, and it is quite dark - very dark, so be careful.<br /><br />Although the only thing i had problem with was how suddenly it ended. But everything was explained, and all pieces fell into place, but even so, i wish epilogue was a bit longer. <br /><br />I want to thank my dear friend <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/10082388-raven-mikhail" rel="nofollow noopener">Raven.mikhail</a> who recommend me the book in the first place! <br />____________________________________________<br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <u>OVERALL</u>
  </i>
</b>: <br />____________________________________________<br /><br /><i>
  <b>This series was really, really interesting, full of great characters and nice fantasy setting. It combines adult type books with a well written fantasy story and makes a perfect balance. </b>

<div id="review_118248681" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/118248681" />
    <a title="Mandi Schreiner" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2704703-mandi-schreiner"><img alt="Mandi Schreiner" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1368979996p2/2704703.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/118248681?book_show_action=true">Aug 23, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mandi Schreiner" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mandi Schreiner" href="/user/show/2704703-mandi-schreiner">Mandi Schreiner</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer118248681" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2414510063160307182">I adore this series and these characters C.L. Wilson has brought to life. She writes the evilest of all villains and the most tortured of all heroes. Between these two men is Ellyseta, a woman so in love with the light, yet marked with evil and teetering on the edge of darkness.<br/><br/>Crown of Crystal Flame, the final book in the Tairen Soul series starts right where Queen of Song and Souls ends. Actually, the prologue is the heartbreaking event of Adrial and his truemate all over again (and their deat</span>
  <span id="freeText2414510063160307182" style="display:none">I adore this series and these characters C.L. Wilson has brought to life. She writes the evilest of all villains and the most tortured of all heroes. Between these two men is Ellyseta, a woman so in love with the light, yet marked with evil and teetering on the edge of darkness.<br /><br />Crown of Crystal Flame, the final book in the Tairen Soul series starts right where Queen of Song and Souls ends. Actually, the prologue is the heartbreaking event of Adrial and his truemate all over again (and their death plays a big role in this book). I don’t know how C.L. Wilson does it, but she gets me so wrapped up in these characters. While I love the story of Rain and Ellysetta, I have become so attached to Bel and Gaelen (part of her guard) and Shan and Elfeya (her parents stuck in prison). She weaves in the stories of her supporting characters to the point I latch on and I don’t want to let go. <br /><br />C.L. Wilson has so much to address and wrap up in this book and I think she does an amazing job. Ellysetta is fighting her four mage marks while Rain is desperate to find a way to finish his bonding before the madness overtakes him. Shan and Elfeya are at wits end after endless torture. Kieran and Kiel are missing with Ellysetta’s sisters. King Dorian and Queen Annoura are struggling in their marriage and constant political maneuverings. And finally, the epic war is on the horizon. Vadim Maur, who may be my favorite villain of all time, has amassed not only a stunning number in his evil army, but has a plan set to capture his prize possession Ellysetta.<br /><br />This book is intense, action-filled and with some absolutely heartbreaking moments that made me tear-up. Everyone’s story, not just Rain and Ellysetta’s, are resolved. Some with joy, others with tragedy. The action starts right from the beginning, and although the actual romance scenes are fewer in this book, there are an abundance of poignant, touching scenes. At this point in the series, we know of the love between Rain and Ellysetta – what we need to see is the final outcome and we are not disappointed.<br /><br />I honestly don’t have any complaints. This book is an outstanding end to one of my favorite series. You must read this series in order, this isn’t one you can casually pick-up halfway through but I highly recommend it. I am not huge into reading fantasy, but this one delivers romance, action and characters that are unforgettable.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2414510063160307182" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText14852997099529091003" style="display:none">What a friggin ride!!!! Not sure about full review to come but something is coming.<br /><br />What an end to an epic ride for me. One of my friends was disappointed with this book and it had me a little worried. I didn’t read the review just looked at the stars and went ut oh. Not at all the case for me. Book 2 was so good I really didn’t expect any of the others to top it but this one did and by a clear margin. Not far in I thought <i>” oh we better not do like 80% more world building and then throw everything at us all at once.” </i> Well that was not the case. It was just the opposite. Don’t want to give the percentage but it is pretty early on that the flood gates opened and there was just no break in the action. It was not stop action even with some more world building going on, although most of that was done on the fly. <br /><br />Very difficult to give a full review on fantasy books but even harder on a book that ties up the loose ends of 5 books. Just read the series it is totally awesome and I am sure I will be heading into a 5 star slide. </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer108836862" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17000179214128184083">Wow, what an ending to a beautiful, epic-like series.<br/><br/>The final book in the story of Rain and Elysseta is powerful, heart-wrenching, riveting and delivered what it promised and more.<br/><br/>I have to admit that during the first half of the book I was literally biting my nails. It is so dark, the enemy so cunning, and the challenges just seemed insurmountable. I was afraid that someone important will die, and I don't think I can handle that. The story, of course, had a positive conclusion, but it was a ri</span>
  <span id="freeText17000179214128184083" style="display:none">Wow, what an ending to a beautiful, epic-like series.<br /><br />The final book in the story of Rain and Elysseta is powerful, heart-wrenching, riveting and delivered what it promised and more.<br /><br />I have to admit that during the first half of the book I was literally biting my nails. It is so dark, the enemy so cunning, and the challenges just seemed insurmountable. I was afraid that someone important will die, and I don't think I can handle that. The story, of course, had a positive conclusion, but it was a ride to get there. <br /><br />Wilson created a complex world with fascinating characters that inevitably wormed themselves into the reader's heart. I was happy for the beautiful ending of Rain and Elly's romance, even as I worried and hurt and fret for them and their friends.<br /><br />I love this series, and highly recommend it to everyone who loves a great romance.</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1243855855?book_show_action=true">Apr 02, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aly is so frigging bored" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aly is so frigging bored" href="/user/show/4290492-aly-is-so-frigging-bored">Aly is so frigging bored</a>

<div id="review_126381453" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/126381453" />
    <a title="Leontine" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2663609-leontine"><img alt="Leontine" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597427167p2/2663609.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/126381453?book_show_action=true">Oct 15, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Leontine" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Leontine" href="/user/show/2663609-leontine">Leontine</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2663609-leontine?shelf=fantasy-romance">fantasy-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer126381453" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17014435579161159042">Some books just rob me of words to adequately describe what it did with me, CROWN OF CRYSTAL FLAME is such a book. C.L. Wilson gave me a conclusion where joy and sadness, love and hate, courage and angst, laughter and tears fuse in to an action filled story that gave me an unparalleled reading experience within the romance fantasy genre. CROWN OF CRYSTAL FLAME is by no means a novel you can read as a stand-alone since it is an end game story where the truemate bond between Elly and Rain needs to</span>
  <span id="freeText17014435579161159042" style="display:none">Some books just rob me of words to adequately describe what it did with me, CROWN OF CRYSTAL FLAME is such a book. C.L. Wilson gave me a conclusion where joy and sadness, love and hate, courage and angst, laughter and tears fuse in to an action filled story that gave me an unparalleled reading experience within the romance fantasy genre. CROWN OF CRYSTAL FLAME is by no means a novel you can read as a stand-alone since it is an end game story where the truemate bond between Elly and Rain needs to find completion or else…, and the battle against High Mage Vadim Maur enters the last stage to claim the final victor.<br /><br />From the first word C.L. Wilson plunged me in to high risk chases and tension filled battles where fey powers and Celierian tenacity clashed with the dark strength of the mages. There is a very fine line between death and survival, defeat and victory, and I can guarantee you there will be moments of angst, tearful goodbye’s and moments filled with utter relief as various characters make it through one ordeal or another. C.L. Wilson holds nothing back, the plot thickens to almost insurmountable heights with a rapid succession of unfolding events. It nailed me to the couch, every major and secondary story thread blended seamlessly together. I was completely absorbed in the story being told as to whether or not my most beloved characters would find peace, joy and love again. <br /><br />The plotlines that were set-up in the former four books of this series and hadn’t found a conclusion do so in CROWN OF CRYSTAL FLAME. The signature beautiful and lyrical writing style of C.L. Wilson encompassed me; it set me on the grim battlefields, it made me soar like a Tairen, weave magic along the fey warriors and allowed me to feel the range of emotions coursing through the characters. This author knows how to bare the souls of the characters, let me witness all the good, the bad and everything in between that they have to give. Each character; Rain, Elly, Belliard, Gaelen, Shan, Elfeya, Vadim Maur, Melliandra, Lillis, Lorelle, the Dahl’reisen and the Tairen, to those new to the series they are just names. Nevertheless, to those familiar with the series know that each brims with a distinctive voice that allows them to come to life via the pages and in the mind’s eye. I loved them all; each of them gave the love, the friendship, the battles and even the darkness of hate or evil meaning and purpose. While the story, as each of the four preceding books, revolves around the completion of the truemate bond between Rain and Elly, it is each supportive character, each secondary storyline, that deepens this series to a rich and multi-layered reading adventure. <br /><br />I cannot tell you much about the story plot itself since each reader who has longed for CROWN OF CRYSTAL FLAME should go in to it unspoiled and experience it all firsthand themselves. The tender courtship romance between Elly and Rain I got to read about in Lord Of the Fading Lands is no longer. Now it is a love, running so deep in the soul of the couple it demands the full and complete truemate bond. There are risks to be taken, the love needs to be expressed, the fear felt and the dangers are everywhere, Rain and Elly’s go rock bottom to aim for the completion of their bond and they took me along with it for every moment! Their romance is truly one of epic proportions that touched my heart to the very core but my heart also plummeted in fear for them and cried for them. This story is the culmination of everything that came to pass and it delivered a breathtaking read from an author who can wholly claim a reader with her characters, imagination, storytelling and high-risk plotting.<br /><br />From the moment I read Lord Of The Fading Lands I knew C.L. Wilson was an author with a fantastic gift for writing. With CROWN OF CRYSTAL FLAME C.L. Wilson has cemented herself among the greatest authors on my shelves with exquisite storytelling, fantastic world building, heart-in-throat tension, larger-than-life characters and a romance that will keep you on edge till the very last chapters. I will love reading this series for the rest of my life!<br /><br />Quote:<br />The Fey did nothing in half measures. That intensity of emotion was part of their appeal. It made them the fiercest warriors, the staunchest allies, the most passionate lovers. The most devoted mates.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17014435579161159042" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_259762907" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/259762907" />
    <a title="Coucher de soleil" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7355786-coucher-de-soleil"><img alt="Coucher de soleil" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1378407561p2/7355786.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/259762907?book_show_action=true">Jan 10, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Coucher de soleil" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Coucher de soleil" href="/user/show/7355786-coucher-de-soleil">Coucher de soleil</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7355786-coucher-de-soleil?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7355786-coucher-de-soleil?shelf=fantasy-read">fantasy-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7355786-coucher-de-soleil?shelf=favorites-2011">favorites-2011</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer259762907" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2587343051368451296">All in all I enjoyed this series. The world building in particular was extremely well done and highly original. I enjoyed the story, the setting, and the characters a great deal. This series was not perfect however and this novel exposed certain problems therein.<br/><br/>Let me also state that this review contains spoilers. If this bothers you, don't read any further.<br/><br/>(i) My biggest issue came towards the end of the book, in which there was a prime example of what I have come to refer to as the TSTL syndr</span>
  <span id="freeText2587343051368451296" style="display:none">All in all I enjoyed this series. The world building in particular was extremely well done and highly original. I enjoyed the story, the setting, and the characters a great deal. This series was not perfect however and this novel exposed certain problems therein.<br /><br />Let me also state that this review contains spoilers. If this bothers you, don't read any further.<br /><br />(i) My biggest issue came towards the end of the book, in which there was a prime example of what I have come to refer to as the TSTL syndrome. :-)<br /><br />This acronym stands for the phrase 'too stupid to live'. I have now come to use this for a book (or movie) where the main character(s) exhibit a highly unbelievable level of stupidity with regards to the eventual actions of the bad guy(s). In this book, the main character's two young sisters are kidnapped by an evil mage, Vadim Maur. As a result, the main character, her mate, and their allies decide to rescue them. However, while even the main characters acknowledge that their plan (which involves using the bad guys' means of travel and assuming they haven't been double-crossed) has more holes than a sieve, it does not really occur to them that the aforementioned evil mage could be waiting for them. And this was the case after said mage had spent most of his time trying to capture the main character which he has become obsessed with (I'm trying not to give too much away here).<br /><br />Um, right. Just how stupid are these people, exactly?<br /><br />(ii) The end of the series is a tad abrupt, insofar as the evil mage is killed very quickly. I will reiterate here what I have said in at least one previous review of another series: while it may be the case that the CHARACTERS need to 'off' the evil character(s) quickly, this does not mean that the written account of this death/elimination needs to be rushed. <br /><br />In the end, the main evil character's death took one paragraph. Frustrating.<br /><br />(iii) The fate of certain secondary characters is left entirely unanswered. One particular character, Melliandra, escapes with one of the Fey women and several children. The two of them, with the children, head for the northern mountains. Nothing more is said about them, which means they've essentially been left hiking forever in a frozen mountain wasteland by the author. <br /><br />I am still hoping this will be dealt with in a subsequent book (the author has said that there will be another novel in this universe, though this novel will not be part of the current series).<br /><br />These elements are unfortunate, because otherwise I truly enjoyed this series and found it extremely well written. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="2587343051368451296" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer2926947253695532189">This is an intense book! So much was going on and so many different places and different people ~ it was kind of hard to keep up with. I think it would have been better to read Queen of Song and Souls(book 4) right before reading this one.<br/><br/>I liked how everything came together and the story of Ellyseta finally being revealed in its entirety. I did feel that it eclipsed Rain a bit but it was understandable. There were some things that were not addressed and some things set up for the spin off books</span>
  <span id="freeText2926947253695532189" style="display:none">This is an intense book! So much was going on and so many different places and different people ~ it was kind of hard to keep up with. I think it would have been better to read Queen of Song and Souls(book 4) right before reading this one.<br /><br />I liked how everything came together and the story of Ellyseta finally being revealed in its entirety. I did feel that it eclipsed Rain a bit but it was understandable. There were some things that were not addressed and some things set up for the spin off books that seem very interesting. <br /><br />I loved the ending! BUT I think it would've been more exciting if you didn't know if there was going to be a HEA or not.<br /><br />I would definitely recommend you reading the books fairly close together. It will be easier to follow and keep track of! </span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=casters-or-witches">casters-or-witches</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=hybrid-multiple-genre">hybrid-multiple-genre</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=elves-pixies-and-fae">elves-pixies-and-fae</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer112395278" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14791487071013978047">Here I am at the end of a wonderful journey to the Fading Lands and back. This is quite possibly, one of the only times that I can recall truly feeling <i>satisfied</i> as I close the book on a series. Not every single question was answered, but I was able to finish the book and relish the magic that was Tairen Soul.<br/><br/>Book 5, the final installment gave me insight into some of my favorite characters like the twins, Kieran, Kiel, King Dorian, Shan, and Elfeya, as well as some of my not so favorite characte</span>
  <span id="freeText14791487071013978047" style="display:none">Here I am at the end of a wonderful journey to the Fading Lands and back. This is quite possibly, one of the only times that I can recall truly feeling <i>satisfied</i> as I close the book on a series. Not every single question was answered, but I was able to finish the book and relish the magic that was Tairen Soul.<br /><br />Book 5, the final installment gave me insight into some of my favorite characters like the twins, Kieran, Kiel, King Dorian, Shan, and Elfeya, as well as some of my not so favorite characters like Melliandra and Annoura. By the end of the story I was even rooting for people I didn't like in the past! I felt the first 100 pages or so dragged a little, but once the book hit its stride, there was nothing but pure bliss in reading. It was fantasy heaven for me. The final battles were so well thought out and described. This book was lighter on the romance/love scenes than the previous books, but surprisingly enough (for me), I didn't seem to miss them. There was just too much going on and so much that I wanted to know for me to worry about if Rain and Ellie were going to get down to business.<br /><br />Will I miss the Fading Lands and the Fey? Without a doubt. I am grateful that Wilson will grace us with spin-off books in the future featuring Bel and Gaelen. My only hope is that we will see appearances from Kieran, Kiel and the twins. So much has been hinted at, but that is the one last thing that I would love to see come to fruition.<br /><br />The only words left to say are this : <i>"Miorah felah ti'Feyreisa!" (Joy to the Feyreisa)</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="14791487071013978047" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_740657822" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/740657822" />
    <a title="Kim  *Mo Chridhe*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9909997-kim-mo-chridhe"><img alt="Kim  *Mo Chridhe*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1431962494p2/9909997.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/740657822?book_show_action=true">Oct 13, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kim  *Mo Chridhe*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kim  *Mo Chridhe*" href="/user/show/9909997-kim-mo-chridhe">Kim  *Mo Chridhe*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer740657822" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3492307394669346554">Overall series rating: 4.5 stars! <br/><br/><b>
  <i>When a Fey warrior meets the woman who completes him, his soul's truemate, he knows in an instant. And in that instant, whether she will have him or no, he binds himself to her, hear and soul with the words "Ver reisa ku'chae. Kem surah, shei'tani," which means "Your soul calls out. Mine answers, beloved." And he spends the rest of their courtship - the rest of his life, if necessary - proving himself worthy of the magnificent gift of her love.</i>
</b><br/><br/>It was a sad, </span>
  <span id="freeText3492307394669346554" style="display:none">Overall series rating: 4.5 stars! <br /><br /><b>
  <i>When a Fey warrior meets the woman who completes him, his soul's truemate, he knows in an instant. And in that instant, whether she will have him or no, he binds himself to her, hear and soul with the words "Ver reisa ku'chae. Kem surah, shei'tani," which means "Your soul calls out. Mine answers, beloved." And he spends the rest of their courtship - the rest of his life, if necessary - proving himself worthy of the magnificent gift of her love.</i>
</b><br /><br />It was a sad, sad day when I finally swiped the last page of this book. To realize that I will never again hear or ever use the words <i>"aiyah", "beylah vo", or "sieks'ta"</i>. Or to feel the thrill whenever I hear <i>"Ku shalah aiyah to nei, shei'tani."</i> I should feel satisfied, and I do. This was a series ender done really well, but not all questions were answered and some important characters just... faded. I feel as though Ms. Wilson set the book up in a way that left us readers hungry for a spinoff. If only to know what happens to Lillis and Kieran, to Gaelen vel Serranis, and to see little Tairen kitlings roaming around the Fey'Bahren. <br /><br />Nevertheless, this series has managed to worm its way to my heart (and my favourites shelf) and guaranteed its spot in my reread list in the future. Despite the cheesy start, I found myself emotionally involved in the characters' plight right away. And though there was a period when my reading kept getting interrupted, I managed to get right back into the story and still continued to be riveted. <br /><br />Rainier and Ellysetta are one of the most awesome couples you will ever read about. Their love and support for each other only grows deeper and stronger with each book. There are beloved characters like Bel, Gaelen and the rest of the quintet who will touch you with their loyalty and their honor as Fey warriors. And then there are those characters who you initially abhor but feel sympathy for later on. The antagonists are threatening, and there is war and conflict, and sadly, death. But there is love, plenty of it. This is truly one of the most romantic series I've ever read! I'm looking forward to getting back to the Fading Lands and reading more Tairen Soul. </span>
  <a data-text-id="3492307394669346554" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer9355518356090308179">Well I'm done and now I don't know what to do with myself. This is an amazingly written series from start to finish and I couldn't recommend it enough to anyone in need of a good fantasy romance read. </span>

I would have loved to see more from this series from the secondary characters.</span>

<div id="review_3367067327" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3367067327" />
    <a title="Roaringwave9" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/110953121-roaringwave9"><img alt="Roaringwave9" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1583428277p2/110953121.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3367067327?book_show_action=true">Nov 02, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Roaringwave9" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Roaringwave9" href="/user/show/110953121-roaringwave9">Roaringwave9</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/110953121-roaringwave9?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/110953121-roaringwave9?shelf=rereadable">rereadable</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/110953121-roaringwave9?shelf=the-onions-got-to-me">the-onions-got-to-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/110953121-roaringwave9?shelf=adult">adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3367067327" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12456262827349338760">This is going to be a review of the series as a whole because I have neither the patience nor the energy to write a review for each book. <br/>I'm genuinely surprised that I reread this series because I don't reread that often and when I do it's usually middle-grade books that I read in middle school and can fly through. It was also surprising because this book contained some tropes that I don't like or rather I should say that they annoy me at times. I did feel like the whole, not like other girls t</span>
  <span id="freeText12456262827349338760" style="display:none">This is going to be a review of the series as a whole because I have neither the patience nor the energy to write a review for each book. <br />I'm genuinely surprised that I reread this series because I don't reread that often and when I do it's usually middle-grade books that I read in middle school and can fly through. It was also surprising because this book contained some tropes that I don't like or rather I should say that they annoy me at times. I did feel like the whole, not like other girls trope was used with Ellie, I definitely felt like Ellie and Rain were forced to be together in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1584974.Lord_of_the_Fading_Lands" rel="nofollow noopener">Lord of the Fading Lands</a>, but that changed significantly by the third book. <br />Okay, now that's out of the way we can move on to the things that I liked about this book. <br /><b>1. The writing</b><br />The writing was amazing if the writing wasn't enjoyable I would not have been able to do a reread, regardless of how much I liked the plot or how attached I was to the characters. The writing style is one of the main reasons why I have been able to do a reread of this while I have not been able to reread some of my favorite series. I will say that the smut scenes especially in the 3rd, 4th, and 5th books were a bit much, but I skipped over them, and they aren't at all vital to the books in my opinion, but that may be because I genuinely don't enjoy reading them.<br /><b>2. The Characters</b><br />I was totally invested in all of the characters, or at least the main characters and their friends. I was scared for all of their lives, and I loved learning the things that I missed on my first read. My heart broke each time one of the fey died. None of the characters felt one-dimensional, I thought that the Eld would be like that at first but as the series progressed I changed my mind. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[This entire series Ellyseta was struggling between good and evil especially after she found out about the mage marks and even before that she was scared of her magic. The same with Rain and all of the dahlreisen. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Just as I thought I knew and understood a character something new would turn up and surprise me, and that is how I feel about people. <br /><b>3. The Plot </b><br />One thing that I totally loved about this series was the pacing, none of the books felt slow, although this book did feel faster than the others, especially at the end. I actually liked that during the war and even before it wasn't just the insignificant characters that died but people who actually mattered to the main characters and the outcome died because that's what happens during a war. Usually when people write war scenes the "good guys" win every single battle and<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ while the Fey, the Celirians, the Elves, and the Danae did win a significant number of the battles in this book and the 4th one the Eld had some victories too. You don't need to win every battle to win the war. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I did feel like some things were a little predictable, but that may have just been because I had already this through once.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12456262827349338760" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_104130156" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/104130156" />
    <a title="Cindi" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1940550-cindi"><img alt="Cindi" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1415082086p2/1940550.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/104130156?book_show_action=true">May 24, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Cindi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Cindi" href="/user/show/1940550-cindi">Cindi</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">fantasy readers, lovers of Bishop, Sterling, Lee and other Fantasy authors</span></div>

        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer104130156" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10266788117837130536">I knew that this series would end on a positive note, but I never could have imagined the path it took to get there. I feel relieved and like I've just emerged from a dark tunnell now that I'm finished. I also feel that "after Christmas letdown". I'm sorry to see it end.<br/><br/>In the Crown of Crystal Flame, Ellysetta is told when everything looks dark, to remember that love is the most important thing. As she and Rain, her Tairen Soul lover and deposed King of the Fey, run from one uprising to another,</span>
  <span id="freeText10266788117837130536" style="display:none">I knew that this series would end on a positive note, but I never could have imagined the path it took to get there. I feel relieved and like I've just emerged from a dark tunnell now that I'm finished. I also feel that "after Christmas letdown". I'm sorry to see it end.<br /><br />In the Crown of Crystal Flame, Ellysetta is told when everything looks dark, to remember that love is the most important thing. As she and Rain, her Tairen Soul lover and deposed King of the Fey, run from one uprising to another, the evil Dark Mages plot and plan to takeover the Fading Lands of the Fey. There is enough action in this book to keep any gamer with a 2 second attention span happy. There is romance if you count the deep and abiding love between Rain and Ellysetta. There are many occurances in this Tolkein-esque tale that should be taken to heart in our day-to-day lives (the dalhreissen are Fey Warriors who have used forbidden magic and are thought to then be honorless and evil; Elly and Rain learn that the Brotherhood of Darkness dalhreissen are not honorless and should never have been outcasts, and allow them to pledge themselves to Ellysetta to regain their honor. Second chances, not believing what was always taught without checking for themselves, and all that).<br /><br />What a great, vast and excellent world Ms. Wilson has built! I hope that she feels the desire to create a break-off series in it, as I am not ready to be done yet.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="10266788117837130536" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer960052800" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1220810775497712919">My rating for the series: <br/>4-stars for Book 1~3<br/>3-stars for Book 4&5<br/><br/>Like:<br/>Originality<br/>Magic <br/>Rain and Fey warriors were awesome!<br/><br/>Meh:<br/>I thought the storyline was in need of a director's cut on some repetitive scenes.<br/><br/>The characters were well-developed, but by book 4, some of them turned into 1-D or 2-D characters that contributed very little excitement to the final installment.<br/><br/>Predictable plot<br/>Lack of twists and turns <br/><br/>The bad people hold the ball and score points while the good guys just play defense! I </span>
  <span id="freeText1220810775497712919" style="display:none">My rating for the series: <br />4-stars for Book 1~3<br />3-stars for Book 4&amp;5<br /><br />Like:<br />Originality<br />Magic <br />Rain and Fey warriors were awesome!<br /><br />Meh:<br />I thought the storyline was in need of a director's cut on some repetitive scenes.<br /><br />The characters were well-developed, but by book 4, some of them turned into 1-D or 2-D characters that contributed very little excitement to the final installment.<br /><br />Predictable plot<br />Lack of twists and turns <br /><br />The bad people hold the ball and score points while the good guys just play defense! I mean it was just damn frustrating!<br /><br /><br /><br /><br /></span>

I was disappointed in the ending of this series.</span>

<div id="review_129642226" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/129642226" />
    <a title="Ronda  Tutt" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2216375-ronda-tutt"><img alt="Ronda  Tutt" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1475858100p2/2216375.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/129642226?book_show_action=true">Nov 07, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ronda  Tutt" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ronda  Tutt" href="/user/show/2216375-ronda-tutt">Ronda  Tutt</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2216375-ronda-tutt?shelf=fantacy">fantacy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2216375-ronda-tutt?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer129642226" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4276427272826046351">Brilliant & Creatively Written!<br/><br/>Just Wow! I am totally blown away. The series is brilliantly written with the world building and the dynasty of connections between the characters. This is one series that imagination and creativity of the plot exceeds any fantasy tale I have ever read. I found myself captivated from the very first book and towards the end of each book I couldn't wait to get to the next book to continue the flowing magical movie like visual of excitement the author’s smooth writing</span>
  <span id="freeText4276427272826046351" style="display:none">Brilliant &amp; Creatively Written!<br /><br />Just Wow! I am totally blown away. The series is brilliantly written with the world building and the dynasty of connections between the characters. This is one series that imagination and creativity of the plot exceeds any fantasy tale I have ever read. I found myself captivated from the very first book and towards the end of each book I couldn't wait to get to the next book to continue the flowing magical movie like visual of excitement the author’s smooth writing revealed as it came alive upon the page.<br /><br />I want to note however that each book is just a part of the story and must be read in order for the reader to understand the awesome plot and the connection between each character.<br /><br />The main characters Ellysetta and Rain are magical and their passion is believable and steam up the pages throughout the series. The fey language will have you melting with heart felt emotions. <br /> <br /><i> <b>“Ver reisa ku’chae. Kem surah, sheitani. Your soul calls out. Mine answers, beloved.”</b></i> (Rain)<br /><br /><i>
  <b>“Whatever your fate, I wil share it. Wherever your Path leads, there, too, walk I. Ver reisa ku’chae. Kem surah, sheitani.” </b>
</i>(Rain)<br /><br />The Tairen creatures are creative as they are a form of great big cats with wings. They are humorous and playful but most importantly they are protective with a fierceness that will have you in awe. Steli is my favorite because of her protectiveness and heartwarming fondness of Ellie, she had me laughing out loud with her humor and actions.<br /><br />The friendship between the Celierian (humans) Fae, Elves, characters bring forth the drama of family history, their fates of religion and beliefs, their turmoil of living and surviving, and their dedication of honor and soul wrenching love to die for.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>“War is a strange thing, kem’jitanessa. I’ve seen bitter enemies fighting side by side, because they hate the thing they’re fighting more than they hate each other. Sometimes you have to take your allies where you find them and hope for the best.”</b>
</i><br /><br />Throughout each book the reader will find the many examples of good (light) vs evil (darkness) and a discovery of how not all evil (darkness) is truly evil but a necessary action of protectiveness and love – a way of life. This is one of the reasons I love about this magical story. <br /> <br /><i>
  <b>“We are all the gods children. All our gifts come from them. It’s what we do with those gifts that determines whether we walk in Light or Shadow.”</b>
</i><br /><br />The evil (darkness) of the Mages along with their demon possessed evil creatures will have you seething for revenge as the torture and graphic bloody scenery plays out in this action packed mystical story. The magical powers bestowed upon the Mages and their minions is bone chilling and will have you gripping the book tight as you read the scenes thinking OMG or WTF. <br /> <br />However, though the reader will be stunned from the horrific scenes of great loss, the passionate warmth of love and good deeds between each book leaves you with a fulfilled contentment up to the final climax of the breath taking Happy Ever After in the end.<br /><br />Overall, I highly recommend this series for all Adult Fantasy fans and this fan of C.L. Wilson looks forward to reading more of her fantastic works. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="4276427272826046351" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('cZNwTs7v/9G8B3K21MIWV9aVJLoRpzwhKXR8FWicM8j2yLVl7aWY95YeHBDXbt7xyUX6MXRSj7i4PiGLBePF/w==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('UV6LxqsfxP1ja8MxFZwebAj66BXHfvNXwUCZajLQ5LDWBU7tiFWj20lyrZcWMNbKFyo2nqKLQM5QCsT0X68Shw==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer27665127272760581">C.L. Wilsons unique blend of pulse-pounding action, sweeping epic fantasy, and passionate romance has made her books a favorite read for romance and fantasy readers alike. Praised for exceptional worldbuilding and lyric prose, her critically acclaimed novels have regularly appeared on bestseller lists including the USA Today, the New York Times, and Publishers Weekly.<br/><br/>C.Ls novels have won numerous </span>
  <span id="freeText27665127272760581" style="display:none">C.L. Wilsons unique blend of pulse-pounding action, sweeping epic fantasy, and passionate romance has made her books a favorite read for romance and fantasy readers alike. Praised for exceptional worldbuilding and lyric prose, her critically acclaimed novels have regularly appeared on bestseller lists including the USA Today, the New York Times, and Publishers Weekly.<br /><br />C.Ls novels have won numerous industry and reader-selected awards including, LifetimeTV.coms Best Paranormal debut of 2007, the Gayle Wilson Award of Excellence, two National Readers Choice awards, the Colorado Award of Excellence, and the Holt Medallion. Ms. Wilson is the honored recipient of the PEARL award from Paranormal Romance as the best new author of 2007, and winner of the 2009 PEARL award for best Romantic Fantasy novel. <br /><br />When not torturing her characters mercilessly, C.L. enjoys relaxing with her family in sunny Florida and daydreaming of a world where people exercise in their sleep and chocolate chip cookie dough ice cream is a fat burning food.<br />"</span>

            <span class="readable">&ldquo;I watch my loved ones weep with sorrow, <br />death's silent torment of no tomorrow. <br />I feel their hearts breaking, I sense their despair, <br />United in misery, the grief that they share. <br /><br />How do I show that, I am not gone...<br />but the essence of life's everlasting song<br />Why do they wee? Why do they cry?<br />I'm alive in the wind and I am soaring high. <br /><br />I am sparkling light dancing on streams, <br />a moment of warmth in the fays of sunbeams.<br />The coolness of rain as it falls on your face, <br />the whisper of leaves as wind rushes with haste. <br /><br />Eternal Song, a requiem by Avian of Celieria<br /><br />from Crown of Crystal Flame by C.L. Wilson&rdquo;</span>
